Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not set, then administer strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of the hip, until it is healed. 
de la dislocation dou talon	Of the dislocation of the heel  
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heel is sometimes strained, and sometimes completely dislocated, both inside and out. 
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee: li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	And the signs are that the ankle is swollen, and taut before the part where it is dislocated; the resetting is gentle, and one should extend the foot gently with their hands when it is relaxed only. 
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville; puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut; et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient; et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide; puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet; puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent; puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	And when it is completely dislocated, you must have the patient sit upright, and hold them firm by the leg, above the ankle; then pull the foot toward you with your right hand, and then with your left twice, then extend it upwards, and push the foot up well; and do this twice, as we have said, by pushing and pulling the foot; if it returns, that is good; if not, start the work again, for it will return; and if it cannot return this way, have the patient lie on their back on the ground, and fix a stick firmly in the ground between their thighs, and tie cloths around, so that they do not hurt the patient; then have the assistants hold the thigh, and another assistant extend the foot with their hands or with a cord, which they tie above the ankle; then each assistant should extend equally, and the stick should be now between the patient's thighs to hold them when it is extended; then place the assistants' hands evenly at the dislocation, and have another assistant hold the healthy leg underneath, and the dislocation will return quickly. 
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And when it has reached its point, apply the plaster and bandages on top, and bind it firmly, and tie the foot to the leg, and guard the nerves which are on the ankle behind so that the bindings are not too tight; then leave it for two days or three, and if the bindings loosen, bind them again; then untie them on the third day or the fourth, and forbid the patient from walking for four days; and if he walks before that time, it is not certain that it will not dislocate again. 
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if an abscess comes, it is necessary that you soothe it, as we have said elsewhere, until it is healed. 
des dois	of two 
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the two are dislocated, if they are nicely extended without effort, it is a light thing. 
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the dislocation is in any joint of the back or foot, it is necessary that you make the patient sit on a level surface or table straight up, and put your foot on what appears of these joints, then press with your foot firmly, until it returns; and when it is equalized, and nothing appears, then put under the sole of the foot a table at two feet, then strain it firmly, and leave it for three days, then untie it; and let it rest until it is healed. 
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wound and of dislocation together 
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	When a wound comes with the dislocation and one wants to restore it, many times it happens that the patient dies: so do not be presumptuous in the cure, if you are not wise in the art and have not used it for a long time, and if you are not pitiful and merciful and slow, do not be bold; and use at the beginning soothing things for hot abscesses, and leave the patient in the hand of God, if you do not see hope of health; and when you see hope, then reset the limb in its place, so that the abscess boils may come; and when the limb is in place, then administer soothing things for hot abscesses, and cure the wound as it befits with drying ointments; and if with the dislocation there is a fracture, and small bones are broken off, set them, and do what we have said in simple diseases; and beware of entering the way of fear, according to what I have said, for this is worth more according to your Creator, and for the safety of your soul and your body. 
Amen	Amen
